The Balkan Situation Worsens: Germany and Italy Eye Greece, British-Romanian Diplomatic Relations on the Brink of Rupture, Romania Reorganizes its Army in Cooperation with Germany

London: Credible sources report that Hitler is currently preparing a joint offensive from the Balkans and Egypt, with the aim of breaking the Mediterranean blockade. The widespread speculation that German General Jodl has been appointed to command the Axis forces in Libya is being taken very seriously. It is apparent that the Italian forces there will continue to advance towards the Nile. (Reuters, 11th)

London: The Daily Mail's Viking correspondent, Mr. Shirto, predicted today that Italy will attack Greece, while Germany is preparing to confront Turkey via Romanian bases on the Black Sea. It is claimed that "I learned today that the Greek ambassador's reply to Romanian Prime Minister Antonescu has postponed this 'sudden change.' During the Brenner Pass Conference, Britain had already prepared for this. However, the serious situation they face is now becoming increasingly clear." (United Press, 21st)

Budapest: News from Bucharest indicates that diplomatic relations between Britain and Romania may be severed within twenty-four hours. German troops have already arrived in Constanța on the Black Sea and will build air and submarine bases at the mouth of the Danube. British personnel at Romanian oil refineries left the oilfields just before the German troops arrived. Italian aviators will soon arrive in Romania to reorganize the Romanian Air Force. (International News Service, 10th)

Yugoslav Capital: German troops conducted large-scale military operations in the Danube River region last night. They passed through Yugoslavia en route to Romania and Bulgaria. German troops have been marching in the Danube area for two days. Coincidentally, a German division recently arrived in Romania by train. Furthermore, it has been learned that German military vehicles passed through the Yugoslav capital in a continuous stream last night. (United Press, 11th)

Bucharest: After hearing the Axis powers' claim that the breakdown of British-Romanian diplomatic relations was only a "matter of time," British officials here began burning important documents last night. At the same time, British sources stated that British diplomats were awaiting instructions from London to prepare to withdraw to Istanbul. The highest Romanian authorities issued an announcement declaring the immediate commencement of the construction of air-raid shelters. Romania is making these preparations in fear that Britain will carry out retaliatory air strikes because Romania allowed German troops to enter the country to protect its oilfields. Meanwhile, Hitler's bodyguard commander, General Rollus, has flown to Galați to inspect Romanian defenses. Last night, diplomatic circles were also discussing completely unconfirmed reports that Germany might pass through Romania and Bulgaria to attack Turkey. (United Press, 11th)

Bucharest: The Romanian cabinet convened yesterday to discuss measures for reorganizing the Romanian army. Plans concerning the construction of barracks, underground defense works, and military highways have now been agreed upon. Conscripts from the 1940 and 1941 classes, originally scheduled to be called up next year, will now be called up early on November 20th. (Haitong Telegram, 11th)

Bucharest: Romanian ministries related to national defense held a meeting yesterday, attended by Prime Minister Antonescu and his chief of staff. Since Romania and Germany have a new military partnership, the plans agreed upon at the meeting are of considerable significance. A communiqué stated that the meeting considered new methods for reorganizing the army and rearming, including building new warehouses to store large quantities of war materials brought by Germany, and building new air-raid shelters in Bucharest. Furthermore, it was decided to call up the 1941 class of reservists for training on November 20th and to take measures to prevent covert military sabotage, with emphasis on aviation. (Reuters, 11th)

Bucharest: It was confirmed here yesterday that Romanian kerosene is now no longer being transported to Turkey and Greece. The motives for implementing this measure have not been explained. (Haitong Agency, 11th)

British Embassy Prepares to Withdraw

Rome: A Haitong News Agency reporter learned from reliable sources yesterday that the British Embassy in Vienna is now packing up everything in preparation for returning home. The British Embassy has also notified British nationals in Romania to prepare to return home quickly at any time. (Haitong Agency, 11th)

Bucharest: Although British nationals in Romania have not received concrete instructions to evacuate, British authorities have urged them to be prepared to leave the country at any time. The British Embassy and British businesses are now making preparations for any sudden changes. Diplomatic circles view the severance of British-Romanian relations as unavoidable, either because German troops may forcefully occupy Romania, or because London will decide that the position of Britons in Romania can no longer be supported. There are at least three hundred British nationals in Romania, and the British Embassy will be responsible for handling the evacuation. Although Romanian Prime Minister Antonescu reiterated his assurance to British Ambassador Hoare on Wednesday night that only small detachments of German troops were ordered to enter Romania, several towns in Romania now have numerous German officers stationed in them, busily arranging encampments and procuring military supplies. The arrogant behavior of these officers has provoked reactions in several provinces, as many leaflets have been found in the markets stating that Romania's inherent rights have been completely sold out. (Reuters, 11th)

Budapest: Axis personnel here expect that the Axis powers will take surprising action in the Balkans within a few days. It is generally predicted that the rapid military action will occur in the Balkans as a result of Germany dispatching troops to Romania and the British Embassy in Romania burning official documents. It is reported that the Italian Embassy in Athens has ordered Italian nationals to evacuate Greece. At the same time, Greek Prime Minister Metaxas and British Ambassador to Greece Sir Palairet discussed the future crisis. It is expected that the number of German troops arriving in Romania this weekend will increase further. The current number of German troops in Romania remains a major question. At the time of the British-Greek talks in Athens, news also came that British air force reinforcements had arrived in Cyprus. It is believed here that if Britain fails to obtain a "satisfactory" explanation from the Romanian government regarding German troop movements in Romania within another day, the breakdown of British-Romanian negotiations seems certain. (International News Service, 11th)

Germans Begin Migration

Budapest: The German consulate here is currently busy repatriating the 170,000 Germans scattered throughout Eastern Carpathia. A mixed Romanian-German committee began discussing the resettlement of 45,000 German minority members from Southern Bukovina here two days ago. The resettlement of German farmers from Bessarabia and Northern Bukovina is being carried out by the German Advance Squad. The first batch of several thousand farmers has set off in trucks, etc., and has now arrived at the port of Galați on the Danube River, from which they will travel upstream along the Danube, passing through the Yugoslav capital and returning to Germany. Another 15,000 Germans will withdraw from Northern Dobruja. However, 250,000 Germans in the Banat province and 350,000 Germans in Outer Transylvania will remain in their original locations. These minority members have already been granted the same rights as Romanians, and can hold important administrative positions in their districts and serve in the Romanian army. Mr. Miller, a British employee of the Astra Romana Oil Company, is still being detained at the police station, but it is said that after an investigation, the authorities are certain that Miller has not committed any acts of sabotage. (Reuters, 10th)

British Planes Continuously Bomb German Nerve Centers Bremen Shipyards Heavily Bombed, Krupp Factory Suffers Major Fire

London: The British Air Force is continuously bombing German nerve centers, almost without interruption, and launched a major counteroffensive on Thursday night and Friday morning, bombing major German targets, including the elastic jumping-off points on the French coast, as well as the "German cannons" bombarding the Dover area for half an hour. Brave British Air Force pilots, braving wind and rain clouds, continued their day and night raids, spreading new destruction across the continent. (International News Service, 11th)

London: The British Air Force raided Bremen in Germany on Tuesday night, heavily bombing the shipyards for an hour and a half. The docks were also repeatedly hit by large bombs, and major fires broke out everywhere. According to the Air Ministry Information Bureau, British aircraft combined the attack on Bremen, dropping high-explosive and incendiary bombs, causing fires to break out everywhere. Also, bombers attacked the Krupp factory in Essen, repeatedly dropping many batches of large bombs on important buildings, causing fires to break out in many places and spread throughout the area, with flames soaring into the sky. At the same time, British bombers separately attacked the invasion ports along the Channel. British aircraft attacking Calais bombed from 8:00 PM onwards, braving thick clouds, until after midnight. (Reuters, 10th)

London: The Air Ministry Information Bureau stated that on Wednesday night, Blenheim aircraft from the British Coastal Command raided Boulogne, dropping three tons of bombs, with a fire breaking out every minute. At one location, a railway station and warehouse near the port of Marie were bombed and caught fire. One pilot saw two clusters of black objects on the surface of the water, seemingly flat-bottomed boats, moored near the wharf, and they were hit by bombs. Also, British naval and coastal aircraft cooperated in attacking Brest, bombing German destroyers in the harbor. Anti-aircraft fire was quite heavy, but these German ships were still inevitably bombed by the central aircraft, and the port's docks and buildings were also damaged. (Reuters, 11th)

London: On Wednesday, the main targets of the British Air Force bombers' night raid were the Krupp factory in Essen, the aluminum factory in Grevenbroich, and the oil storage depot in Cologne. Other targets, such as the railway traffic in Rotterdam, Amsterdam, Vlissingen, Le Havre, Calais, and the German-Dutch border, were all bombed. Two major fires broke out in the factory area ten minutes after the Krupp factory was bombed. British aircraft attacked the Grevenbroich aluminum factory for two hours, dropping approximately ten tons of high-explosive bombs and hundreds of incendiary bombs, causing the factory to be hit, explode, and catch fire. (Reuters, 11th)

London: An Air Ministry communiqué stated that British bombers bombed German oil supplies and transportation lines, other military targets, and the invasion ports in German-occupied territory on Thursday night. (Reuters, 11th)

London: The Air Ministry announced that on Thursday evening, British bombers attacked oil depots, transportation routes, and other military targets within Germany, and also bombed various invasion harbors within the German-occupied areas. (Reuters, 11th)

London: German radio news reported that British planes attacked Amsterdam again on Thursday evening, destroying many houses and causing many deaths and injuries, and claimed that there were no military targets near the attacked locations. (Reuters, 11th)

London: The British Air Force heavily bombed the Krupp munitions factory in Essen for two hours last night in heavy rain and snow, dropping a large number of bombs. An oil refinery north of Cologne caught fire. Railway warehouses, docks, and cargo ships in Boulogne were all destroyed by fire. (Reuters, 11th)

US Government Authorities Discuss International Situation, Especially Emphasizing Pacific Problems, US Chargé d'Affaires to Berlin Recalled

Washington: US President Roosevelt met with Secretary of State Hull and Undersecretary of State Welles at the White House yesterday afternoon to discuss the current tense international situation. According to President Roosevelt's secretary, Mr. O'Leary, the president discussed general international situations, including various developments that could affect the situation in the Far East. He stated that senior government officials would continue to hold talks and make various discussions on the situation abroad, but Mr. O'Leary declined to express an opinion on which political situation the government authorities were particularly concerned about, but stated that the recent talks covered a very wide range. At the same time, State Department officials stated that the US Chargé d'Affaires to Berlin had been recalled home for consultations and would not return to Germany. The US Consul in Berlin will replace Mr. Kirk as Chargé d'Affaires, while Mr. Kirk, according to authoritative reports, will be appointed Chargé d'Affaires to Rome, as US Ambassador to Italy Phillips is currently on sick leave. The State Department has repeatedly stated that Mr. Kirk's recall does not have any significant political implications, and is merely a matter of routine. His appointment as Chargé d'Affaires to Rome is a temporary measure to deal with sudden changes. It is understood that President Roosevelt's meeting yesterday was due to the recent developments in the Dutch East Indies, which have attracted the President's attention. President Roosevelt also met with non-official personnel. After Pan American Airways manager Mr. Waldner told the press that he believed the situation in the Dutch East Indies was extremely serious, he was summoned by the President. According to Mr. Waldner, "Japan's demands on the Dutch East Indies and its 'New Order' plan have created an absolutely serious situation." He believes that the US taking a firm stance can counter the war in the Pacific. Pan American Airways has negotiated with the Dutch East Indies government authorities regarding the establishment of an airline route from Batavia directly to Manila by Pan American Airways. Revisions to the Regulations for the Bereavement Support for Government Troops

Chongqing: Regarding the cases of bereavement support for army officers and soldiers killed or wounded in action, the authorities, in order to simplify procedures and expedite the bereavement support, have slightly revised the regulations for bereavement support, which have been submitted to the National Government for record and implementation. The main points of each regulation are recorded as follows: (1) Cases of commendation and those that must first be submitted by the Military Affairs Commission to the Executive Yuan and then submitted to the National Government for publication shall still be handled as usual. (2) All cases of peacetime and wartime death in action, death on official duty, death from overwork, and death from injury during the War of Resistance shall be handled in accordance with the provisions of the Provisional Regulations for Bereavement Support for the Army in Peacetime and Wartime, and the Military Affairs Commission shall first fill out and issue the bereavement orders. (3) At the end of each month, the Military Affairs Commission shall compile a survey table listing all cases of bereavement support and send it to the Executive Yuan for submission for record. The cases of bereavement support for the navy and air force shall also be handled in accordance with the above methods. (11th Dispatch)

Sichuan Gentry Voluntarily Donate Military Grain

Chongqing: A dispatch from Wan County reports that Mr. Shi Zhuxuan, a local gentry residing in Chongqing, responded to the military grain donation movement by dispatching his eldest son, Shi Shanwu, back to the county. He donated one thousand shi of this year's newly harvested grain to the local authorities to help with military supplies at the front. The administrative commissioner of this district, Min Yonglie, and the county magistrate, Yang Fu, took stock. Min and Yang telegraphed the provincial government to request commendation. Many local gentry in this county have also recently voluntarily donated grain to the county government. (11th Dispatch)

It is reported that Mr. Huang Juming, a gentry in Lu County, took the lead in donating 200 market shi of military grain, followed by You Zijun who donated 30 market shi. Shi Shanwu from Wan County donated 500 shi, Chen Youyu and Yu Shaocheng each donated 400 shi, Yu Mengzhe and Guo Hankai each donated 300 market shi, Huang Junfu donated 200 market shi, and Chen Songyao and Liu Yingsheng each donated 100 market shi. The Chinese National Day After Three Years of Struggle: The Understanding That the Chinese People Should Have

Today, twenty-nine years ago, under the great leadership of Dr. Sun Yat-sen, the Father of the Nation of China, and the generous sacrifice of countless martyrs who died for the country, China was able to overthrow the imperial system and establish a republic. On this Double Tenth Festival in this year when major changes are unfolding in East Asia and the world, the Chinese people, recalling the achievements of nation-building in those years, must deeply understand the goals of the Chinese revolution and nation-building, continue the spirit of the revolutionary martyrs, and do their utmost to fulfill their current great tasks. The goal of the Chinese revolution and nation-building is to realize Dr. Sun Yat-sen's Three Principles of the People, on the one hand, to seek China's independence and freedom, and on the other hand, to promote the great spirit of China's inherent morality, to restore China's national status, and to promote peace and happiness for all mankind. China's founding in East Asia naturally requires first seeking peace and stability in East Asia, and only by ensuring the stability of the Pacific can there be a reliable guarantee of world peace. Therefore, Dr. Sun Yat-sen's lifelong struggle, which is also the great ideal of nation-building of the Xinhai Revolution, is nothing more than strengthening national defense internally to seek China's freedom and equality; and stabilizing Asia externally to achieve true world peace.

However, the Japanese side fears the completion of this goal of the Chinese revolution and nation-building, because their consistent attempt is to control East Asia and conquer the world. If China's nation-building is completed and becomes strong, their attempt will be impossible to achieve. Therefore, the Tanaka Memorial not only says, "If you want to conquer the world, you must first conquer China," but also says, "The most frightening thing is that China is becoming increasingly aware. In the future, when China is unified, industry will inevitably develop accordingly. Therefore, it is necessary to actively seize rights in Manchuria and Mongolia, and then use Manchuria and Mongolia as the command tower to seize the benefits of all of China." This is not just Tanaka's words, but the basic national policy of the Japanese side. Since the Xinhai Revolution, Japan has continuously interfered with and undermined China's unification, economic recovery, and national defense construction. After the Northern Expedition of the National Revolutionary Army, the attempt to obstruct China's nation-building became even more obvious. From September 18th to July 7th, they launched a large-scale attack on China. China, unable to endure it any longer, rose up to survive. The struggle of more than three years is actually to strive to realize the ideal of nation-building, and also to complete the cause of the Xinhai Revolution and realize the Three Principles of the People. It must achieve the goal of restoring sovereign independence and territorial and administrative integrity, and it must also achieve the goal of establishing international credibility, human justice, and world peace before it can be said to have completed the revolutionary mission. "Only justice in the world can never be extinguished, and justice will surely triumph over power." The Chinese people must have a thorough understanding of this on the Double Tenth Festival commemorating the founding of the nation.

Japan's attempts are not concealed by themselves. The Tanaka Memorial blatantly said: "Japan wants to use China's resources to conquer the Indian Ocean, Asia Minor, and Europe"; and also said: "Japan must fight the United States and the Soviet Union." Their so-called "New Order in East Asia" is to have all the countries in the Pacific submit to Japan's power and recognize it as the sole master of Asia. China understands this, so it is not only determined to fight to crush its attempt to conquer China, but also to break its dream of conquering East Asia. China is the oldest and largest country in East Asia. Without China, there is no East Asia, and the security of East Asia is deeply and closely related to China's survival. Therefore, China is determined to take the lead in stabilizing East Asia.

Since the European War, Japan has seen an opportunity and has advanced the "New Order in East Asia" to the "Greater East Asia Co-Prosperity Sphere," vainly attempting to take advantage of the danger to actively advance southward. Recently, it has even concluded a tripartite alliance. This policy of going against the tide is actually an expression of its inner anxiety. China must do its best to cope with it for the sake of self-defense and nation-building. China will never tolerate the so-called "New Order in East Asia" or "Greater East Asia Co-Prosperity Sphere." Any country that recognizes Japan's "leading position in Greater East Asia" will regret it one day. Because any treaty concluded with Japan regarding East Asia that is opposed by the Chinese people will be equal to a piece of waste paper and cannot have any effect. Japan's intention is really to use this tripartite alliance to end the "China Incident." As long as China perseveres to the end and never yields, this attempt will surely be shattered.

Looking back at the environment in which the pioneers of China's nation-building were in during the Xinhai Revolution, their difficulties were no less than today's, and what they relied on was less than one ten-thousandth of what the Chinese soldiers on the front lines have today. However, they were not afraid of death and never turned back, and finally created the Republic with bare hands. As Dr. Sun Yat-sen said: "In the Battle of Huanghuagang, 300 people fought against more than 30,000 people, using pistols and bombs to resist long guns and artillery; as for the Wuchang Uprising, one person fought against 500 people. This kind of struggle is not found in the art of war in ancient and modern China and abroad, and only the history of revolution has this precedent." If the Chinese nation wants to survive in the world forever, it must follow the spirit of the martyrs, and like them, give their lives to serve the country and sacrifice everything. Only in this way can the goal of revolutionary nation-building be achieved. The spirit of those who experienced thousands of dangers, broke through thousands of difficulties, endured hunger and cold, and worked hard in the independence of the United States, the revolution in Soviet Russia, and the revival of Turkey can also be used as an example for the Chinese people.

China's current struggle is indeed entering a difficult stage, but it is much better than the environment at the time of the Xinhai Revolution. Because China is only fighting against one opponent, and all the countries in the world that love justice are friends of China. Everyone hopes that there will be an independent and strong China in Asia. Everyone anticipates that the development of the new China after victory will help the world's economic cooperation and help establish true world peace. Therefore, as long as the Chinese people themselves are confident and work harder from now on, any external resistance will not be an obstacle to the completion of the goal of revolutionary nation-building.

China's war from beginning to end is based on the position of self-reliance and self-strengthening, and strives independently to carry out its firm goal. Therefore, no matter how the international situation changes, it will be beneficial to China and will not be affected by it in the slightest. Recently, the assistance of various friendly countries to China has become more active, and the sanctions against Japan have also become more intensified. This is indeed beneficial to China's war, but the biggest intangible significance is that the evolution of the international situation is getting closer and closer to the purpose China has embraced day by day. Dr. Sun Yat-sen's ideal of saving the world will surely be recognized by the world in this great world turmoil, and will eventually be fully realized. As long as the Chinese people have confidence, any environmental difficulties can be overcome. It is necessary to work hard when the international situation is favorable, and even when the international situation is unfavorable, we must still fight to the end. Future history has already destined China's nation-building to be a success.

Chairman Chiang Kai-shek once said on the Double Tenth Festival in 1937, "This war cannot be ended in a year and a half." Now, three years after the struggle, China's arduous struggle has been connected to the final liquidation before the world obtains the final light. The Chinese people should feel that they are truly shouldering heavy responsibilities, so they must have greater courage and patience, and more hard work and diligence, to engage in the sacred work of nation-building. The Chinese people must know that all the nation-building codes that Dr. Sun Yat-sen painstakingly taught in the past were anticipating such a once-in-a-lifetime opportunity today; they must take the following three points as preparations to encourage themselves to act: (1) Concentrate their will, enrich the Republic of China, and lay a sound political foundation. (2) Develop industries, increase production, and strive for research and creation to lay a solid and independent economic foundation. (3) Work hard to train, revitalize industry, improve weapons, develop transportation, and lay the foundation for the national defense plan set by Dr. Sun Yat-sen.

The people of the whole country of China, especially the leaders with knowledge and skills, recognize that the responsibility for China's revival and the responsibility for the rise and fall of East Asia and the prosperity and decline of the world are all on their shoulders. This responsibility cannot be avoided. They must stand firm and achieve the greatest and greatest cause with the determination of utmost loyalty and bravery, so that they are worthy of being the successors of Dr. Sun Yat-sen and the revolutionary martyrs, and continue the solemn mission to the nation, ancestors, East Asia, and the world.

Education News

Amendment to the Regulations on the Establishment of Free and Publicly Funded School Places at All Levels (Below)

(Article 13) If schools at all levels concurrently set up free places and publicly funded places in accordance with these regulations, the publicly funded places shall be given to students from poor families with better entrance examination results or academic performance in school. If the number of new students and students in school who apply for free or publicly funded treatment exceeds the number of free or publicly funded places that each school should set up, each school shall give its free or publicly funded places to students with better entrance examination results or academic performance in school.

(Article 14) If the conduct and academic performance of a student who receives free or publicly funded treatment are on average below Grade C, the school may suspend his free or publicly funded treatment. The detailed measures shall be determined by each school at its discretion.

(Article 15) The granting of free and publicly funded places by schools at all levels shall be jointly reviewed and determined by the principal appointing several faculty members to form a committee (called the Free Places Committee or the Free and Publicly Funded Places Committee) to show openness and prevent favoritism.

(Article 16) The fees for students who are granted the publicly funded places set up by schools at all levels in accordance with these regulations shall be determined by each school in accordance with local living conditions and reported to the competent educational administrative authority for record.

(Article 17) If free and publicly funded students at schools at all levels are found to have falsely claimed to be poor or forged certificates of poverty, the school may recover all fees from the student or his guarantor and may suspend the issuance of transcripts or diplomas. If any personnel participating in the review of qualifications are found to have committed any acts of favoritism or deception, they shall be subject to disciplinary action.

(Article 18) The education departments and bureaus of each province and city and public and private colleges and universities shall, within two months after the beginning of each academic year, report the progress of handling free and publicly funded places to the Ministry of Education for record.

(Article 19) The various scholarship places set up by each school, the expenses of which come from public and private agencies, groups, or individuals, and are not paid from the school's regular budget, shall still be generously maintained and shall not be used to offset the free places or publicly funded places stipulated in these regulations. (Article 20) These regulations shall be implemented from the date of promulgation.

Hong Kong Government Plans to Establish More British Children's Schools in Australia

(Hong Kong Correspondence) The Hong Kong government has always paid special attention to education. In addition to the government's public schools at all levels, it also allocates more than 17,000 pounds of funding to subsidized private schools every year. Over the years, it has cultivated many talents. However, since the situation became tense last year and the evacuation of women and children was carried out, the impact on education has been enormous. Most of the school children who receive government subsidies every year have been evacuated to Australia and other safer British colonies. After this group of school children was evacuated to Australia, because the number of people was too large, the local schools could not accommodate them as much as possible, and the transfer procedures were very troublesome, resulting in the vast majority of them dropping out of school. At the same time, the evacuation of school children in Hong Kong has caused the following problems: (1) Teachers who used to work in schools have lost their jobs due to the suspension of school affairs due to school children leaving school. (2) Indirectly affecting the income tax levied by the government on teachers' salaries is a serious issue.

Shanghai Middle School Student Roster Deadline at the End of the Month All Documents Must Be Universally Reviewed

In terms of education in this city, in accordance with the Shanghai Wartime Secondary School Student Status Reorganization Measures approved and implemented by the Ministry of Education, all public and private secondary schools in the city are ordered to create and submit rosters of new students, transfer students, and continuing old students from the first term of the 29th academic year, and to keep the admission documents of new students and transfer students until the end of each semester before returning them, so that personnel can be sent to review them. It has already been detailed in various newspapers. It is now known that most of the student rosters of various schools have been sent, so the review of student status documents will begin today based on these rosters, school by school. In addition to the fact that various schools should provide as much convenience as possible to the student status review personnel who hold proof documents, they should also number the documents of each student in advance to facilitate verification. The period for creating and submitting student rosters should have ended earlier, but for the sake of flexibility and convenience, it has been extended to the end of this month. Late submissions will not be accepted. The schools that have not created and submitted rosters will be published in various newspapers at the beginning of next month, so that the students of each school will know that the student status of their school has not been submitted to the Ministry of Education, and it will not be recognized. (Dahua News Agency)

Daylight Saving Time Ends in All Schools in This City

According to education officials, the daylight saving time movement was decided by the Public Works Bureau to be suspended from midnight on the 12th of this month. All schools in this city will move back one hour from midnight tonight, and classes will resume at the same time as before June starting Monday. (Dahua News Agency)

Jiangxi Province Increases the Salaries of Elementary School Teachers Monthly Pay of Five Dou of Grain

(Ji'an Correspondence) The Jiangxi Provincial Department of Education, in accordance with Chairman Chiang Kai-shek's order to increase the salaries of elementary school teachers, inspected the local situation and stipulated that the insurance teachers in all counties of the province should uniformly allocate five dou of grain per person per month from the county (a total of six shi per year). If it is temporarily impossible to raise funds, they may borrow accumulated grain from township granaries to distribute it, and return it after the autumn harvest next year. It has been ordered to all counties to implement it from this semester.

金融　外匯回緊

Yesterday's foreign exchange market saw the HSBC listing remain unchanged. The British and American exchange markets showed a tightening trend, reflecting the slight easing of the relationship between Japan and the United States. Foreign banks increased their purchases, initially softening the market to 3.75 and 5.78125, but Chinese banks and speculators sold heavily, and the Bank of Japan also intervened. The tightening trend soon subsided, and the market entered a period of consolidation, closing at 3.8125 and 5.875, a tightening of 0.015625 and 0.125 compared to the previous day.

Chinese Merchants Still Selling

The morning opened with London telegraphic transfers down 0.0625 for both near and far terms. New York silver prices remained stable, London gold spot prices were fixed, and the exchange rate for the pound against the US dollar was unchanged, but against Shanghai, it rose 0.1875. The US dollar fell 0.075 against the pound and rose 0.27 against Shanghai (all compared to the previous day). The Central Bank's listed exchange rates remained unchanged. Banks opened with spot selling prices of 3.78125 for the pound and 5.875 for the US dollar, a decrease of 0.046875 and 0.125 respectively compared to the previous day. The opening favored brokers who were eager to buy, and a certain American bank also made purchases. Although Chinese merchants took the opportunity to sell, the market continued to soften, with trades opening at 5.875 and 5.8125 for the current month's US dollar. Spot prices tightened to 3.75 and 5.78125. The HSBC listing remained unchanged, and the silver parity tax was down 0.005. Subsequently, Chinese merchants continued to sell, and the Bank of Japan also suddenly showed a willingness to sell. Foreign banks gradually reduced their purchases, and the market rebounded. Trades opened at 5.875 and 5.90625 for the current month's US dollar. At the same time, Chinese banks also sold US dollars for October delivery at 5.90625 to foreign banks. After 10:30 AM, Chinese banks bought current month's US dollars from Chinese merchants at 5.9375. At this time, spot prices also loosened to 3.828125 and 5.9375 for settlement. By noon, sellers had decreased, and the market stabilized, with closing prices of 3.8125 for the pound and 5.90625 for the US dollar.

Market Sentiment Changes in the Afternoon

In the afternoon, Hong Kong cables began to sell, initially slightly tightening the market, selling the current month's US dollar to foreign banks at 5.9375. At the same time, speculators also sold at this price. However, traders suddenly changed their minds and bought current month's US dollars from foreign banks at 5.90625, softening the market. Later, it was difficult to settle the current month's contract at 5.90625. By the evening close, the pound remained at 3.8125 and the US dollar at 5.875. The pound for November delivery was at 3.796875 and the US dollar at 5.84375. The current month's contract tightened 0.015625 for the pound and softened 0.125 for the US dollar compared to the previous day.

補空雖起　金市所漲尙微

Although short covering emerged, the gold market's gains were still minor.

Yesterday, the black market for cash gold improved, mainly because the relationship between Japan and the United States in the Far East had slightly eased. This caused some operators to change their minds, covering their short positions at low prices, buying relentlessly. However, because money exchange firms and banks continued to sell short, the rebound was not overly strong. The market closed at 5,570 yuan, an increase of 65 yuan compared to the previous day. After the close, the off-market was firm, reaching 5,585 yuan. The total trading volume for the day was approximately 3,000 taels. Jewelry stores raised the price of gold jewelry by 10 yuan, while customs gold remained flat.

Cash Gold Rises 65 Yuan

The market opened 35 yuan higher than the previous day due to the slight easing of the situation in the Far East. Gold shops offered 30 taels of gold at 5,540 yuan. Subsequently, the market fell back 10 yuan due to some selling by money exchange firms and securities firms. Securities firms and banks each offered 10 taels of gold to jewelry stores, retreating to 5,530 yuan. Later, the exchange rate tightened, and a certain gold firm actively bought, and banks also bought at this time. The market soon rose to 5,595 yuan. Subsequently, the exchange rate softened, and money exchange firms aggressively sold short at high prices, while buyers cautiously observed. In addition, banks turned around and sold, and the market soon fell to a low of 5,505 yuan. Later, the exchange rate slightly tightened again, and a certain gold firm's buying interest revived, and securities firms also followed suit. The market rose again to 5,580 yuan. However, before the close, buyers decreased, and money exchange firms and floating profits were released, resulting in a closing price of 5,548 yuan. The market opened in the afternoon with jewelry stores purchasing 20 taels from money exchange firms at 5,560 yuan. Shortly thereafter, bulls from gold firms suddenly sold slightly, immediately falling to 5,535 yuan. Subsequently, securities firms and banks competed to buy, and the market rebounded to 5,570 yuan. Later, because a certain bank tended to sell short and money exchange firms also sold, the market retreated again to 5,550 yuan. Afterwards, the market rose to 5,575 yuan before the close due to securities firms and another bank competing to buy. The evening close was 5,570 yuan, an increase of 65 yuan compared to the previous day. After the close, the sentiment was stable, and the off-market traded at 5,585 yuan. The total fluctuation was 90 yuan. The selling price of cash gold from cash gold shops was more than 10 yuan higher compared to cash gold, and the purchasing price was reduced by 30 yuan. Current margin gold was more than 50 yuan lower than the listed gold price, and there were few trades.

Gold Jewelry Listed 10 Yuan Higher

The exchange rate for gold jewelry was listed 10 yuan higher at 9:30 AM, and there were no changes thereafter. Da Tong Hang revised the listing to 570 yuan, and the prices of Xin Tong Hang were similar to the previous prices. Purchases were reduced by about 30 yuan.

投機詩話

Speculative Poetic Talk

- Hu Yimeng

This time, due to the rumors of the evacuation of American expatriates from the Far East and the reopening of the Burma Road, the foreign stock market plunged due to public anxiety. Many people went bankrupt, which is enough to serve as a warning to those who are infatuated with foreign stocks and addicted to speculation. However, I am also one of them. Ten years of hard work were lost in an instant. In a state of utter boredom, I had no choice but to dip my brush and write poems to express my resentment, to give to my fellow enthusiasts, and to warn them for the future.

Ode to Foreign Stocks (Tune: Waves Washing Sand)

Betting on foreign stocks for gold and silver, a piece of paper as evidence, the sudden rise of a downward trend is truly frightening. Locked deep in an iron box, unable to open, it is heartbreaking to see. War clouds rise in East Asia, causing fear and panic, paradise is about to turn into a concentration camp, regretting that I lightly valued fiat currency in the first place, bringing groans of pain upon myself.

The Norwegian campaign caused a wild crash in foreign stocks, which could not be salvaged. The market had just turned better last week, but unexpectedly, due to the current situation, it collapsed again. I wrote this with a heavy heart! (Seven-character Quatrain)

A weak branch, barely sprouted after frost,

Skillful manipulation has initially restored its former glory,

The sound of reed pipes rises on the Pacific Ocean,

Overnight, the west wind scatters flowers again.

A Glimpse of the Market on October 9 (Seven-character Quatrain)

The short covering failed last time,

Today, there is no one to buy the sold-off shares,

I advise you to wash your dragon-slaying hands,

And quietly watch the sunset clouds over Jiangdong.

紗花　多空見解不同　紗市迴旋

Cotton yarn - Divergent views between bulls and bears, the yarn market revolves.

The yarn market is still in a revolving state. Currently, there are divergent opinions in the market. The buyers say that raw cotton is firm, expensive, and bullish. The sellers say that foreign exchange rates are easing, there is a large stock of yarn, the situation is tense, and it has already risen by 400 yuan since the low point, so it may fall back a little. Therefore, the two sides are arguing fiercely. Today, 1,175 pieces of cotton yarn were shipped to Hong Kong and 55 pieces to Yantai.

The market for current yarn opened with good sentiment. Buyers in the market were in high spirits. The price of 20-count Shuangma yarn was 1,170 yuan. Subsequently, it was heard that Japanese yarn was mediocre, and foreign exchange rates shrank and then rose again. Therefore, although the calls were loud, there were few new buyers at high prices, and the market turned downward, falling to 1,162 yuan. However, some scalpers came out to cover their shorts, and the market improved slightly. By the time the market closed, it was still flat. The transaction volume for half a day was 4,270 bales. The price of 10-count Shuangma yarn fell by 10 yuan. The amount of purchases by each gang is listed below.

棉市靜寂

The current cotton market remains sluggish and lacks excitement. However, most people are bullish, still believing that the sources of supply cannot be opened up, and the inventory will gradually decrease and become weaker. However, Japanese factories have little intention of operating. Only trading between colleagues is more lively.

Another news report on foreign cotton prices: The New York cotton market was slightly weak, first due to a lack of buyers, then due to quieter spot trading, and pressure from the stock market on Wall Street. As a result, the market closed down 8-9 pounds compared to the previous day. Indian forecasts fell by one rupee.

Shanghai Foreign Cotton Trading: Trading has not been active in recent days due to the shortage of inventory on the market and the sluggish prices of cotton yarn. Most peers are in a wait-and-see attitude. As a result, factories have no cotton to buy. The market is unusually quiet, but prices remain firm.

糧食　洋米銜接而來　新粳亦小一二元

Grains - Imported rice arrives in succession, new japonica rice also down slightly by one or two yuan.

Imported rice arrives one after another. The Taikoo Company's Suzhou ship arrived in Shanghai from Hong Kong the day before yesterday (National Day), carrying 5,609 bags. Also, Jardine Matheson's Fusheng ship arrived on the same day, also carrying 4,189 bags from Hong Kong. Another 660 bags were transferred to Qingdao and shipped on the original ship yesterday. Yesterday, Jardine Matheson's Yongsheng ship arrived at the port, carrying 501 bags from Hong Kong, unloading at the Roosevelt Wharf. The Taikoo Company's Qingyuan ship also arrived in Shanghai yesterday, carrying 1,621 bags from Hong Kong, unloading at the company's wharf in Pudong (Zu).

The inventory of imported rice is sufficient, and fixed loans and sources of supply are continuous. With the foreign exchange market flat, new foreign transactions have been planned for a long time, and the Nanyang issue and the friction between Britain, the United States, and Japan are not enough to arouse the interest of importers. Speculators lack the opportunity to stimulate the market and are mostly waiting and seeing, waiting for the opportunity to disrupt the market again. Therefore, the market was very quiet yesterday, falling by a small half yuan in the morning. In the afternoon, Changyi, on behalf of China South Enterprise Company, sold 1,000 tons of Saigon No. 1 rice at a price of only 75.5 yuan, also down 0.70 yuan from the 76.2 yuan before Double Ten Festival. Public sentiment tended to soften, and there were no buyers for the original package rice returned to the market. The current market price of imported rice has continued to fall by one yuan, a total of one and a half yuan lower than the close on Wednesday evening.

More than 3,000 bags of new japonica rice have arrived. Sales are declining due to the weakness of imported rice. Therefore, the selling price is 1-2 yuan lower than before the anniversary. Minhang new japonica rice is 78 yuan, Xitang Baixue rice is 80 yuan, Qingjiao Dujian rice is 68 yuan, and Taicang imported rice is the only one that is selling well due to lack of supply, selling for 66-67 yuan.

The market for broken japonica rice is about to run out. Only Nangang early rice continues to open high, from 81-82 yuan to 76-77 yuan.

National glutinous rice is also scarce, and foreign goods are very popular, so the prices of national goods are stable while the prices of foreign goods are depreciating. The price of Jinli special rice still needs about 72 yuan, and the price of Hong Kong special rice has already dropped to about 71 yuan, eventually dropping to 68-69 yuan.

現粉軋缺　門售無貨應市

Cash flour is in short supply, and there is no stock for sale in stores.

Yesterday, the current flour was still in short supply. Because the amount allocated by each factory was limited, the actual sales in the street increased due to the addition of wheat flour, and there was often a shortage of supply. Most stores currently have no stock for sale, and a small amount of imported flour is used as a substitute, so imported flour is also in short supply. Shuangying brand is 18.7-18.8 yuan per bag, and the retail price of Fushou brand is as high as 19.6 yuan. However, the purchase of returned old car brand warehouse warrants and Chinese factory flour customers has not changed due to the large orders of imported flour, remaining at 18.4-18.5 yuan.

Wheat - The market was as quiet as ever yesterday. In recent days, the sources of supply from various places have been at firm and expensive production prices, and the costs have been high, so there has been no wholesale shipment to Shanghai. It is even more difficult to import into the concession, so sellers are thinking of supporting the prices, but manufacturers have no intention of lowering prices for purchases. The result is still original plate sporadic embellishment.

Due to the high price, the sales of the lower-grade, all-yarn riding breeches fabric are stronger than in previous years. The imported riding breeches fabric market is slightly better due to limited inventory. Silk and Tea: Japanese and American Silk Prices Rise Frequently, Limited Rise in Local Prices

The day before yesterday was the Double Tenth Festival and the market was closed, but American and Japanese silk prices continued to rise. New York spot Japanese silk rose by one dime to one dime and one cent, Shanghai silk rose by six cents, and Guangdong silk rose by eight cents. Yesterday, New York silk prices were firm and flat, with spot and forward prices rising by six to six and a half cents compared to the previous market. Yokohama had no market yesterday. Considering the futures and spot prices on the ninth, prices rose by forty yuan and nineteen yuan compared to the previous day.

The local silk market could have sailed smoothly and started an upward trend. However, the situation in Japan and the United States also affected the exchange rate, so the rise in silk prices was limited. White filature B-grade silk was sold at prices ranging from 5,100 yuan to 5,150 yuan, nearly 100 yuan higher than at the beginning of the week. It is said that a few transactions were made with British and French foreign firms for export to the United States, due to the impact of regulations and the lack of goods available on the market.

Ten cases of tea will be shipped to Hong Kong today (the 12th), and another 510 cases will be shipped to Tianjin.

China's Post-War Silk Industry (Continued) (10th)

— Shi Xiang

(B) The Silk Market's Adversity

The silk market this year gradually declined. Since the end of the spring silkworm season, it has become even more unstable. The impact of the European War has affected the entire silk industry. In New York, prices have been falling daily. New silk entering the market has encountered adversity. For example, in mid-June, in the New York market, 13-15 denier silk reached US$2.75 per pound. By August, it had fallen to US$2.45, a drop of US$0.30 per pound (equivalent to a drop of US$40 per picul of silk, which weighs 133 pounds). Although the current market situation has improved slightly, most of the silk from small factories has been sold out, so we are no longer the ones profiting.

At that time, the issue of shipping raw silk arose again. Those who had sold to foreign firms in Shanghai beforehand were unable to deliver the goods. Because of the difficulties in shipping, most of them sold on the spot. However, the selling price was 500 yuan lower than that of foreign firms in Shanghai. Local silk merchants, seeing that manufacturers urgently needed funds, often lowered the selling price. At one point, only 1,000 yuan could be advanced in cash after weighing each picul of silk, and the remaining amount could only be collected after a delay of twenty days. Because manufacturers were facing imminent deadlines for payments in the countryside, they sold at a loss to solve their immediate needs. At that time, the highest price per picul of silk was only 4,000 yuan, which meant a loss of at least 970 yuan per picul. The calculation is as follows:

The price of fresh cocoons is 390 yuan per picul. After drying, this yields 280 catties. Adding 60 yuan for expenses, the price of dried cocoons per picul is 1,152 yuan. To reel one picul of raw silk requires 380 catties of dried cocoons. Therefore, the cost of one picul of silk is 4,377 yuan. Adding 600 yuan for reeling labor (i.e., production costs), the cost of each picul of silk is 4,977 yuan. However, it is now only sold for 4,000 yuan, resulting in a net loss of 977 yuan per picul. (To be continued)

Page 9

Bloodshed in Hongkou Yesterday Morning: Rumors of Xiaoan's Assassination and Death, Tragedy Born from Within as Old Servant Murders with Knife, Japanese Side Conducts Major Search but Finds Nothing

At 4:30 AM yesterday morning, a sudden assassination occurred at No. 26-2, Xiangde Road, at the intersection of Shigaota Road in Hongkou, shocking the area. The deceased was "Shanghai Mayor" Fu Xiaoan. It is said that the previous day was the Double Tenth Festival, and he reportedly went to the "City Government" in the morning to preside over the celebration ceremony. He gathered with relatives and friends somewhere in the evening, and returned home late after enjoying himself. Two hours after he fell asleep, he was killed by his close attendant Zhu Sheng with a sharp kitchen knife. It is rumored that he was stabbed three times, hitting the eye, jaw, and neck. The neck wound was the most fatal. After completing his objective, the murderer sneaked out of the mansion and disappeared without a trace. It is said that the Fu family has offered a reward of 50,000 yuan to capture the murderer. Anyone who provides information leading to the arrest will be rewarded with 25,000 yuan. Although Japanese soldiers and "city police" were dispatched on a large scale afterward, they found nothing.

Those Around Fu Talk About the Cause of Death

According to those around Fu, his death must have political implications, "because he was too humble and did not agree to go to Nanjing to take office." Fu usually had strict security, employing as many as 23 guards, and Japanese soldiers and "city police" were stationed outside his residence. Fu had recently told people that he was planning to resign. Unexpectedly, he was killed by the servant he trusted most in his family. Moreover, according to a Mr. Wu, a member of Fu’s circle, told Western reporters that prior to the Nanjing Committee appointing a successor, the current state of the "City Government" could only be put on hold,

The Residence's Security Was Extremely Tight

Fu, named Zongyao, courtesy name Xiaoan, was 69 years old (born in 1872) and a native of Zhenhai, Zhejiang. His Shanghai residence was previously at No. 1, Xingfu Lane, Lubaan Road in the French Concession, before moving to No. 1189, Xiafei Road. The house was purchased from a German at the lowest price during the First World War. He now resides at No. 2, Lane 26, Xianglu Road, Hongkou. He had one wife and one concubine. His first wife, Zhu, died of illness on November 25th of last year. She bore him one son and one daughter each. His eldest daughter is married to Zhu Zigui, manager of the Bank of Communications. His second son, Pinggui, is 46 years old and serves as the chief auditor of the China Exchange Bank. Pinggui's wife has nine sons and four daughters. His grown sons have also had three sons, one of whom is studying at a Japanese kindergarten. Fu's concubine, Zhang, is from North China and has been elevated to the status of wife. Fu's residence usually has extremely strict security, with more than 20 "shock troops" deployed, guarding the house day and night.

Three Fatal Wounds, Died on the Spot

Fu employed many male and female servants, but Zhu Sheng was the most trusted. Zhu, courtesy name Shengyuan, also known as Chen Zhongnan, was 42 years old and a native of Shandong. When Fu was wanted and fled to Dalian, Zhu was hired at a monthly salary of 22 yuan. Zhu has a mistress who lives somewhere on Nanjing Road. He usually either goes home or, when there are events taking place inside the residence, he stays in the “guard room.” The previous day was the Double Tenth Festival. Fu gathered with relatives and friends until midnight before returning, and fell asleep exhausted. At 4:30 AM yesterday morning, Zhu suddenly obtained a kitchen knife and entered Fu's bedroom to assassinate him, slashing at Fu's head three times, hitting the eyes, jaw, and throat. The wounds were extremely deep. Seeing that his objective had been achieved, Zhu abandoned the knife and fled.

Japanese Soldiers Dispatched, Searching Pedestrians

At this time, Fu's wife, Zhang, woke up in a start and entered the room to investigate. She found Fu dead in a pool of blood, and became terrified. The guards downstairs then learned of the incident. After receiving the news, the commander of the Japanese Naval Landing Forces immediately dispatched a large group of armed soldiers to search pedestrians in the Hongkou area and implement a lockdown. They also went to Zhu Sheng's residence somewhere on Nanjing Road to search, but Zhu Sheng's wife had moved away three weeks earlier. The Shanghai Municipal Police Department also dispatched a team of detectives to the scene after receiving the report. However, after finding out that Fu's residence was outside the Public Concession, they turned back midway. According to the English-language "China Press" newspaper, this morning (the 11th), when Fu was killed in his bedroom, there were two Japanese and White Russian bodyguards in the neighboring room. However, they did not hear any sound when the bloodshed occurred. Today, it was said that when the murderer left Fu's residence, a servant of a nearby Chinese family saw his hurried appearance and asked him about it. The murderer said that he had resigned because he had not received his wages.

Trains on Both Lines Were Even Cut Off

After Fu was assassinated, in addition to implementing a special curfew in Hongkou, the Japanese side even ordered the suspension of trains on the Shanghai-Nanjing and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo railways, hoping to arrest the murderer. It is noted that Fu took office as the so-called "Mayor of Shanghai" on October 16th, 1938, and it would be almost two years since then. In March of this year, he once went to Japan. He had once celebrated the first anniversary of his so-called "inauguration" last year, but the celebratory archway suddenly collapsed in a hurricane. It was said that this was an ominous sign, which has now come to pass. Fu was recently scheduled to visit Japan again for the "East Asia Metropolitan Alliance Conference," scheduled to depart on the 24th of this month, but he was killed before he could go.

Extraordinarily Prominent During Sun Chuanfang's Time

Fu had a humble background and only later became prominent. He successively served as the Director of the Gaochang Temple Manufacturing Bureau in Nanshi, the Shanghai Supervisor of the Bank of China, the General Manager of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company, a High Advisor to the Ministry of Finance, the Director of the Shanghai Customs Clearing Office of the Ministry of Finance, the Chairman and General Manager of the Shanghai Commercial Bank, the General Manager of the Siming Bank, and the President of the Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce. He was extraordinarily prominent during Sun Chuanfang's time. When the National Revolutionary Army pacified Jiangsu and Zhejiang, Fu was wanted and fled to Dalian, Japan. After the outbreak of the Sino-Japanese War, he secretly returned to Shanghai. He took office as "Mayor" on October 16th, 1938. It is said that Fu's body will be embalmed and lie in state at his residence for several days before the funeral.

Fu Assassinated

It has been found that there were four attempts to assassinate Fu. The first time was a few months after he took office in 1938, when he was suddenly shot at by a guard, but luckily was not hit. The second time was at a banquet at the International Hotel last year, when someone attempted to assassinate him at the table, but he escaped unharmed. The third time was a few months ago, when Fu was holding a Buddhist service at a temple on Gordon Road to commemorate his deceased wife, Zhu. He was attacked by a monk, but the attempt failed. The monk was caught by the guards and executed. Yesterday morning was the fourth time, when he was hacked to death by a trusted old servant. It seems that his fate was predestined. It is said that Fu's body is currently still lying in his residence.

Jiang Tianduo Passes Away in Beiping, to be Commended, Jiang Lived a Pure and Self-Respecting Life, Kong Xiangxi Sends 1,000 Yuan in Condolences

After Mr. Jiang Tianduo, who held important positions in the former Beijing government, passed away in Beiping last month, the central leaders deeply regretted his integrity and uprightness during his lifetime. In addition to Deputy Prime Minister Kong of the Executive Yuan sending 2,000 yuan in condolences, it is rumored that the government will issue an official commendation to promote encouragement. Jiang was a native of Huaxian, Guangdong. He studied in Japan in his early years and graduated from the law department of Waseda University. He joined the Tongmenghui and participated in the revolutionary movement. After the founding of the Republic of China, he was elected as a member of the first National Assembly. He successively served as the Vice Minister of Agriculture and Commerce, Vice Minister of Justice, Minister of Agriculture and Commerce, Minister of Justice, and President of the Water Conservancy Bureau in the former Beijing government. His entire family resided in Beiping. After the establishment of the National Government, he performed miscellaneous tasks in Shanghai. After the outbreak of the Sino-Japanese War, both the North and the South enticed him with "high positions," but he firmly refused and maintained his integrity. Last month, he rushed to Beiping to take care of his ailing mother, but suddenly contracted a serious illness and passed away at the age of 61.

Shanghai-Hong Kong Route: Dangerous Areas, Announced by the Hong Kong Navigation Authority, Including Nine Locations Such as Xiangshan Port

The Hong Kong Shipping Administration announced the following dangerous areas between Hong Kong and Shanghai: (1) Dangerous areas for shelters, including Xiangshan Port, Sandu Ao, Laiyuan Bay, Ersha Bay, Nanwan Port, and Xinghua Bay. (2) Dangerous areas for underwater power drift, namely Haitan Gorge (between Ai Near Reef and Flag Island to Shuangzu Island). (3) Potentially dangerous areas, namely Biwan Port and Luqing Bay. Safety cannot be guaranteed in these areas. All navigators must consider the mine area and the possibility of floating mines. They must wait for changes in the weather before setting the course. All shipping companies operating on the Shanghai-Hong Kong route have followed this directive.

Allegations of a Run on American Banks: Entirely Groundless, Busy with Deposits and Withdrawals Before and After the Holiday, Business Flourishing and Prosperous

Rumors have circulated that following the U.S. State Department's public announcement advising the families of American nationals in the Far East to evacuate as quickly as possible, American nationals in Shanghai were rushing to withdraw their deposits from American banks. Inquiries from various sources have confirmed that these rumors are untrue. According to a senior staff member of a certain bank, the increased volume of deposits and withdrawals before and after the holiday is a normal phenomenon and nothing to be concerned about. Amidst the current volatile situation, banking business is in fact flourishing and prosperous. Some members of the Chinese propertied class are exchanging U.S. dollars for legal tender, while others are exchanging legal tender for U.S. dollars, buying and selling according to their individual needs. According to general opinion among the Chinese, the State Department's proposal to evacuate American nationals from the Far East is a sign of an increasingly assertive U.S. policy in the region. Consequently, the value of legal tender has suddenly risen.

The U.S. Expedites Evacuation Work, First Group to Depart Next Month, Shanghai East American Community Notified by Consulate, Dependents of Naval Officers Also to Return Home

Since the United States adopted a firm stance to maintain its interests in the Far East, the Japanese attitude has gradually softened. However, according to several foreign diplomatic personnel, the situation in the Far East has not eased due to Japan's softened attitude. This can be seen in the Shanghai U.S. Consulate's handling of the evacuation of American nationals. The U.S. Consulate is continuing its evacuation work. According to a unique source of information from authoritative American sources, the dependents of key U.S. naval officers in Shanghai have also confirmed dates for their evacuation back to the United States.

First Group of Americans Scheduled to Leave Shanghai

Although President Roosevelt has not strongly confirmed the evacuation of non-essential American nationals in China, the U.S. Consulate General in Shanghai received notification from the State Department on the 8th of this month. Yesterday morning, reporters learned from American sources that the consulate is seriously handling the evacuation. The consulate has already issued notices to the first group of registered American evacuees, explaining the contents of the State Department's instructions. The second batch of notices will be issued within days. Most of the first group of Americans preparing to evacuate reside in the eastern district of the International Settlement. The U.S. Embassy will provide subsidies to the impoverished or middle-class employees and their families to facilitate their return home. According to a New Life News Agency reporter, a group of American women and children are scheduled to return to the United States on the American President Lines' President Coolidge on November 6th.

American Organizations Hold Meetings to Discuss

Since the American Association and the American Chamber of Commerce have received instructions from the State Department in Washington regarding the evacuation of American nationals from the Far East, including North China and Shanghai, the two organizations found it necessary to discuss the steps they should take and how they should assist the authorities in carrying out the evacuation. The American Chamber of Commerce held a meeting yesterday afternoon and made detailed decisions on how to dismiss lower-paid American employees. The American Association will be convened by Chairman Fett in the next two days. It is said that both organizations believe it is necessary to increase the number of ships to the Far East for the evacuation and will request this from the authorities.

British Nationals Not Preparing to Evacuate

The British government's attitude toward its nationals in the Far East or China is of great concern to all circles. According to the British Consulate General, the British government has not yet issued such instructions, and the responsible parties have no plans to evacuate. When asked whether it would be necessary to evacuate British nationals in the future, those in charge said that the British government in London had not issued any evacuation notices and did not wish to comment.

U.S. Military Withdrawal Undecided

U.S. Secretary of the Navy Frank Knox's statement in Washington about withdrawing 1,600 soldiers from the Asiatic Fleet and the Fourth Marine Regiment stationed in China has not yet been finalized. However, the strengthening of the defenses of key U.S. naval and military bases in the Pacific, such as Manila, Subic Bay, and Hawaii, is indeed due to the escalating situation in the Far East. In the event of a possible withdrawal of the U.S. Navy in Shanghai, since Shanghai is an international settlement, it is unlikely to undergo drastic changes like in the First World War in 1914, and its neutral status will undoubtedly be maintained.

French Concession Strengthens Military Force, Reorganizes Volunteer Corps and Special Police, Assists Garrison in Responding to Military Actions

The French Consul General's office believes that the current situation has changed and the Concession is facing pressure. For this reason, it has reorganized the Volunteer Corps and the Special Police. The main points of the reorganization are as follows:

French Volunteer Corps

(1) The French Volunteer Corps of the French Concession was established in 1897 and reorganized in 1938. This reorganization is the fourth. (2) According to the new organization, all current members of the French Volunteer Corps must formally join the corps after registering. However, this is limited to those who support the Pétain government or are under French protection. Foreigners of nationalities other than French who wish to join the Volunteer Corps must have resided in the French Concession for many years, possess property, and have passed an examination by the authorities to prove their military knowledge. (3) The Volunteer Corps is organized into a regiment, consisting of A: an active regiment and B: a reserve regiment. Active duty personnel, after passing the new registration and examination, must have training in the operation of new weapons, possess military knowledge, and be well-intentioned towards the Pétain government. (4) The Volunteer Corps has one commander (currently the director of the education department of the French Municipal Council, Gu Loubao), one deputy commander, and several non-commissioned officers. (5) Weapons include heavy machine guns, light machine guns, grenade launchers, mortars, armored vehicles, automatic rifles, and pistols. (6) In the event of military action caused by foreign parties, the Volunteer Corps will assist the French garrison in Shanghai and act in concert. (7) The Volunteer Corps has never had a fixed number of personnel. Among them, 147 White Russian volunteers are incorporated into the French Police Department as paid mercenaries.

Special Police

(8) The issue of Special Police is now being reorganized due to the withdrawal of a majority of British and American residents. The structure includes one chief inspector, one secretary, and 14 inspectors, with a total of 135 personnel. The task of leading and managing is to inspect the service status of non-French personnel in the police stations and other agencies when military action occurs in the French Concession, and to investigate their rebellious behavior.

Shipu Bombed for the First Time, Japanese Aircraft Drop Eight Bombs, Destroying Over 300 Houses

At 9:45 a.m. on the 9th, four Japanese aircraft were spotted over Haimen. The Ningbo air defense observation post issued a series of emergency air raid alerts. The Japanese aircraft then attacked Shipu, circling twice.

Bombing

A total of eight bombs were dropped, including two incendiary bombs. One incendiary bomb landed in Jiangxin Temple, two bombs were dropped on Wenfu Street, one bomb landed in Tiger Cave, and one bomb landed in the river outside the West Gate. Three civilians were injured: a man, a woman, and a child.

Over 300 Houses Destroyed

After dropping the bombs, two of the aircraft fled towards Songkan, Fenghua, Ningbo, Cixi, and Guanhaiwei, while the other two flew towards Hengshan and Chuanshan. The all-clear was sounded at 10:50 a.m.

Four Foreign Ships Detained in Shenjiamen Released, Baoli Arrives in Shanghai, Moufu Trial Voyage Canceled

Begin Unloading Today

To Zhoushan Island

Nie Zhongcheng Public School Buildings to Be Returned on Schedule, School Likely to Reopen Next Year, Jewish Refugees Trying to Find Accommodation

According to the English-language Greater Shanghai Evening Post, the Shanghai Municipal Council's Nie Zhongcheng Chinese Public School on Jingzhou Road, which was leased to the Jewish Immigrant Committee and housed 2,000 German Jewish refugees, is to be vacated by the Jewish Immigrant Committee by November 1st, in accordance with the terms of the lease. Nie Zhongcheng Chinese Public School is expected to reopen next year. However, it is not known whether classes will be held at the original school on Jingzhou Road. It is said that the Municipal Council has sold the school property to a certain Japanese real estate company, but this has not been confirmed. At the same time, the Immigrant Committee has no concrete plans to accommodate these 2,000 Jewish people. It is rumored that some of them will move to the Pingliang Road refugee camp. However, most Jewish immigrants plan to do business in the central part of the International Settlement, and the Pingliang Road refugee camp is too far away to satisfy them.

National Day Celebrated with Enthusiasm, Public Organizations Wire Respects to Chairman Chiang, Support National Policy to Complete the Great Cause of Revival

On the National Day holiday the other day, all sectors of society believed that the current National Day coincided with the evolution of the international situation, which was more beneficial to the military resistance against Japan. In addition to the usual holiday celebrations, all institutions, public organizations, schools, shops, and residents hung flags to celebrate. The brilliant national emblem fluttered throughout the city, and the atmosphere was exceptionally enthusiastic. All sectors also worked together to support the national policy and complete the great cause of national revival, intensifying their efforts in their respective positions, accelerating the promotion of thrift and savings, and the winter clothing donation campaign. The National Day winter clothing donation campaign will last until the 17th of this month. Therefore, the charity sales of shops and individual thrifty donations will continue to be promoted to complete the goal of collecting winter clothing before the 31st of this month. On National Day, public organizations and others sent telegrams to the highest leader and frontline soldiers to express their condolences and respect.

Joint Alert Lifted Yesterday

The authorities of the two settlements, in order to prevent accidents, began a joint alert on the 8th. Now that the anniversary has passed safely, it was announced to be lifted yesterday. The defense forces of various countries and the Shanghai Volunteer Corps were all demobilized. The embassies and consulates general of various countries in Shanghai, such as the United States, Britain, France, Germany, and Italy, all took a day off on October 10th to commemorate the anniversary of the Republic of China and celebrated accordingly. They resumed office yesterday and have announced this to all residents and the public. Many foreign shops in Shanghai also took a holiday to celebrate the Double Tenth Festival and resumed business yesterday.

Overseas Air Mail Routes Slightly Changed, Divided into Four Lines Via Hong Kong

The airmail routes from Shanghai to foreign countries have been slightly changed. The details are as follows: (1) Royal Airlines (Hong Kong via Bangkok to South Africa and Hong Kong via Bangkok to Australia) transports to Indochina, Siam, Malaya, Burma, India, Iraq, Africa, Dutch India, and Australia. (2) United Airlines (Hong Kong to San Francisco) transports to the Philippine Islands, Java, Hawaii, Britain, Canada, Central America, South America, and Europe. The plane departs from Hong Kong once a week and arrives in San Francisco in seven days. (3) He Yin Airlines (Saigon via Hanoi to Sydney) transports to Dutch India and Australia. It waits for ships to Hong Kong for transfer to Saigon. (4) Shanghai to Japan Air Route. All airmail is sealed and sent at 20:00 every day. All mail to the Americas, with the corresponding airmail postage, is transported using this route. It is shipped from Shanghai to Japan, connecting with ships from Yokohama to the Americas, and is then noted to transfer to various European countries via Liberia. The corresponding airmail postage can also be added. As for airmail to the above-mentioned places, it is all sent from Shanghai to Hong Kong by ship, so the delivery time will be slightly extended.

New Radio Circuit Directly to Cuba, Global Wireless Telegraph Company Opens Today

It is known for its excellent service and efficient work. It is now announced that a new direct circuit to Cuba has been opened today (the 10th) to facilitate the public.
