Daylight Saving Time Ends at Midnight Today, Clocks to Be Turned Back One Hour

The Shanghai daylight saving time, which has been in effect since June, has been participated in by all sectors and has achieved satisfactory results. It has now been announced by the authorities that it will end at midnight today. Starting at midnight today, all sectors will follow the regulations of the authorities and uniformly turn back their clocks by one hour. According to a reporter from the New Life News Agency, starting tomorrow, post offices, courts, public organizations, shops, and other organizations will resume their original working or business hours. The public buses and trams in the two settlements will all return to their pre-June 1st departure and return times. The power company will resume testing fire at 4:00 p.m. at the old time. The curfew will also be changed to the old time of 12:30 a.m. In addition, the silver and money industry has also decided by the two associations that from the 14th (Monday), business hours will return to the old time of 9:00 a.m. to 4:00 p.m. All banks and firms have complied. It is heard that the daylight saving time has benefited individuals, families, and society. The authorities have decided that it will be held every year in the future.

Public Transportation in the French Concession Halted Again Yesterday, Temporary Employees Prevented from Going to Work, All Sectors Intend to Mediate Negotiations Without Success

Since the drivers and ticket sellers of the French Water and Electricity Company went on strike, they temporarily recruited more than 200 workers and apprentices to fill the positions of the strikers and maintain the operation of the trams. However, these people mostly lived in Nanshi and went out early and returned late. For two weeks, there had been no obstacles. Unexpectedly, yesterday morning, when they went to the Luban Road tram depot from Nanshi, they were suddenly prevented from going to work by the striking workers. In addition, more than 50 people in the engine room of the company who had not participated in the strike and all the workers in the machine affairs office were forced to join the strike. As a result, all trams and public buses in the concession were completely suspended. It is said that all the striking workers gathered in a certain place in Nanshi yesterday afternoon and held a meeting to discuss methods of negotiating with the capitalists.

Mediation Fails

It was found that the company's workers went on strike on the 25th of last month and agreed on 16 conditions, requesting the capitalists to respond. Because the conditions had to be translated into French, the capitalists were unable to respond immediately. On the 30th, the labor side again proposed six preconditions, requesting Yu Qiaqing and Yuan Ludeng to present them to the capitalists when mediating the labor dispute. On the 2nd of this month, the labor side again requested mediation from the political affairs department of the French police station. The capitalist side also responded to three of the labor side's conditions on the same day. The labor side then carried the revised conditions for negotiation the next day. The capitalist side was unable to send anyone to attend for some reason, causing the negotiations to come to a standstill. Although relevant parties intervened to mediate, it was not successful in the end.

Points of Contention

It is also learned that the labor side's demands are still to insist on the six preconditions proposed on the 30th of last month. The first item is that "the capitalist side recognizes the union and pays office expenses of 400 yuan in national currency per month," while the capitalist side only recognizes the old union. The second item is that the 28 workers and striking workers who were unjustly detained in the case of inspector Chen Tongzhang must be released unconditionally. The capitalist side stated that the power to release the arrested workers was in the hands of the police station, and the company could not make any decisions. The opinions of both sides on the other items, such as the third item of increasing wages, the fourth item of increasing doorkeepers, the fifth item of not dismissing workers without cause, the sixth item of paying wages during the strike period, and the payment of retirement funds, are still close. Therefore, if the labor side can make concessions on the first and second items, the entire labor dispute can be resolved easily.

Concern from All Sides

It was stated by the authorities that they still hoped that the political affairs department of the French police station and influential people in society would come forward to mediate. As for the livelihood of the striking workers, it is said that rice has been distributed to the families of the workers. It is also learned that the political affairs department of the French police station and the Chinese directors of the Public Concession, Yu Qiaqing and Wei Tingrong, etc., considering that the matter is expanding and hindering social security, will quickly seek a proper solution.

Security at the Depot

After the trams and public buses in the French Concession were completely suspended yesterday morning, the labor unrest became more serious again. The main gates of the company's depot and machine workshops on Xujiahui Road, etc., have also been open as usual since the strike, and various workers repairing vehicles have also been working as usual. Yesterday, however, barbed wire was erected at the intersection of Luban Road and Kangti Road, and more than a dozen French and Vietnamese police officers were stationed there to prohibit all pedestrians and vehicles from passing through. Residents who want to enter Luban Road must enter through other roads from Xujiahui Road. A gap was left in the middle of the barbed wire for the company's employees and patrolling motorcycles to enter and exit. A gun carriage was parked at the door of the depot inside the barbed wire, and the doors of all the factories were locked, showing a rather serious situation. However, the general situation is still peaceful. It is heard that on the night of the Double Tenth Festival, a large number of transport workers and ticket writers disappeared from the Sixteenth Shop. At the same time, when a driver living at No. 192-282 Kangnao Road was having dinner at home, ten people suddenly came and dragged him out of the house. The driver was in a hurry and sounded the police whistle, which allowed him to escape.

Continued Negotiations

According to the English-language Greater Shanghai Evening Post, the strike of 2,500 workers of the French Tram Company has lasted for seven days and has not been resolved. The 200 drivers and ticket sellers who maintained the main line business also suddenly stopped working today (the 11th) and joined the strike. According to Mr. Fa Fulei, the manager of the French Tram Company, this morning, the labor and capital sides are still continuing negotiations, but he was unable to announce any definite news about the labor unrest. The main line business of public vehicles in the French Concession continued as usual this morning, but after foreign employees of the tram company repaired the wires at the intersection of Gongguan Road and Balizhao Road, the public buses were completely suspended at around 8:30 a.m. It is heard that after the labor side put forward seven demands on the 7th of this month, the labor unrest was close to resolution, but these demands were rejected by the capitalists. It is believed that the expansion of the labor unrest today, and the suspension of the main line business of trams and public buses, is due to the capitalists rejecting the demands. However, although the labor unrest spread again this morning, no accidents or disturbances occurred.

No Worry About Water and Electricity

After the workers in the engine room of the French Water and Electricity Company went on strike yesterday morning due to past disputes between the engine room workers and the White Russian workers, which the factory had not satisfactorily resolved, they also left the factory and joined the strike. The work in the copper shop and the coin shop was announced to be suspended. A part of the waterworks workers was also implicated. After the company received the news, it immediately summoned the White Russian workers to the factory to take over, so the engine opening and the waterworks were still operating as usual, and there was no worry about water and electricity supply. The company paid great attention to it and was prepared.

Incidents of Robbery Recorded

At 12:00 noon yesterday, in room 104 of the Hardoon Building on Nanjing Road, four robbers suddenly appeared. Two of the robbers took out guns to threaten the people and robbed more than 900 yuan in legal currency and more than 50 yuan in old Japanese bills before leaving.

Last night, a Western woman was walking along Baina Road in Shanghai when she was suddenly stopped by two robbers with guns. The robbers snatched the woman's handbag and tried to escape. The woman immediately shouted for the police to catch the robbers. The robbers turned back and fired four shots at her to warn her. The woman lay on the ground to avoid being hit. Fortunately, she was not hit. The robbers escaped without a trace with the stolen goods.

Japanese Warships Bombard Zhenhai Port, 86 Shells Fired

According to the Zhejiang Provincial Association in Shanghai, the following telegram was received from eastern Zhejiang yesterday: (1) At 8:35 a.m. on the 9th, three Japanese warships outside Zhenhai Port suddenly fired 38 shells at Jiangnan. At 8:55 a.m., they fired 14 shells at Dongmen. A shell landed on a civilian house at No. 102 Dongmen Road, injuring one person and destroying one house. A shell landed on the Xu family's house in the third bao, destroying one house. A shell landed on No. 52 Dongmen Road, also destroying one house. Shells landed on No. 50 and No. 18, destroying two houses each and injuring one person. Two shells landed in Haiyundi, destroying two houses. Four shells landed in Yingdeguan, destroying three houses. Two shells landed in front of the Yu family's house, destroying two houses. A shell landed in Zhenhai Middle School, destroying one house. Four shells landed in the Houhaitang suburbs, with no known losses. (2) At 4:51 a.m. on the 9th, three Japanese warships anchored outside Zhenhai Port fired ten shells at Jiangnan and 38 shells at Zhenhai Dongmenwai. The shells landed in the barren countryside and mud, and we suffered no losses. (3) Three Japanese warships anchored off Shipu left one to the north on the 9th at dawn. The remaining two warships also fired 15 shells at Shipu without any markings at 8:16 a.m. At 9:30 a.m., the two Japanese warships also sailed north, but their destination is unknown.

Trial Implementation of Money Exchange Business: Foreign Currency Buying and Selling Exchange; Limited to the Bank Area East of Shanxi Road; Clearing Twice Daily

The Shanghai Money Exchange Trade Association, recognizing the increasing prevalence of theft and the extreme danger faced by members carrying funds for collection and settlement, is initiating a trial operation of a foreign currency buying and selling exchange. If the trial is successful, a formal establishment will follow. All member firms of the association are eligible to join as members of the exchange. Trading hours are as follows: morning transactions conclude at 12:00 PM, with members submitting their transaction details by 1:00 PM. After reconciliation, members are notified by 2:00 PM. Afternoon transactions conclude at 3:00 PM, with members submitting transaction details by 4:00 PM. After reconciliation, members are notified by 5:00 PM to settle accounts. Transactions after 3:00 PM, whether conducted within the exchange or independently, are settled on the following day.

Geographic boundaries are defined as follows: north from the southern bank of Suzhou Road to Henan Road, south to Avenue Edward VII, west from Shanxi Road, and east to the Bund. Transactions outside this area will not be settled through the exchange. Members outside this area must handle collections themselves. The exchange is located within the Trade Association. Members participating in the exchange must record the buying and selling of gold notes, noting quantities. Members must record the firm, price and quantity of both buy and sell transactions separately. Summaries should be sent to the exchange within the specified time, for total reconciliation and notification of required settlement. Those delivering funds must send them to the business address of the recipients.

Massive Copper Theft Case Involving Two Million Yuan: Perpetrator Escapes; Suspect Hides in Broadway Mansions; Police and Japanese Police Cooperate in Attempted Arrest; Japanese Military Police Firmly Request Leniency

The English-language China Press reports that Swiss national Whittle has been wanted for stealing five hundred tons of copper worth two million yuan from the premises of the American trading company Swan, Culbertson & Fritz, copper that was being transferred from the American firm's godown at the godown of the China Forwarding and Storage Company. Yesterday (the 10th) at 11:00 AM, a constable from the Shanghai Municipal Police and two officers from the Japanese Consular Police went to the seventeenth floor of Broadway Mansions

to arrest Whittle.

They were suddenly stopped by Japanese military police. It is understood that several years ago, the Swan, Culbertson & Fritz sold coin-minting machinery to the Chinese government, and received five hundred tons of copper in payment, all packed in crates and stored in the godown of the China Forwarding and Storage Company. It was recently discovered that the copper had been stolen, and the crates had been replaced with sand. It was then discovered that Whittle had orchestrated this largest theft case. Before the theft, trucks had been seen driving to the godown at night, and then

driving to Hongkou

District. The Swiss Consul-General, upon learning of the situation, issued an arrest warrant ten days ago. However, Whittle was hiding in Hongkou, making it difficult for the Shanghai Municipal Police to arrest him. On the 10th, it was learned that Whittle was in his apartment in Broadway Mansions. A constable from the Shanghai Municipal Police, together with two officers from the Japanese Consular Police, went to the address to make the arrest. Whittle contacted his lawyer, Toune, by telephone, who then contacted the Japanese Military Police. A squad of armed Japanese military police arrived at Broadway Mansions and

firmly requested his release.

As a result, Whittle, the perpetrator of the massive theft, escaped. It has been reported that Whittle has previously been imprisoned twice for privately selling firearms and committing fraud. Furthermore, according to reliable sources, regarding the case of Swiss national Whittle stealing copper worth two million yuan, the Swiss Consul-General in Shanghai, Fontanel, stated that he was studying the steps to take, but could not comment at this time. American authorities also intend to initiate an investigation into this case, as the companies involved, Swan, Culbertson & Fritz, and China Forwarding and Storage Company

are both American

firms. It is believed that Whittle is still hiding north of the Suzhou Creek. It is understood that the Shanghai Municipal Police has given up the pursuit, but if he enters the Public Concession south of the Suzhou Creek, he will be arrested. Sources believe that the Swiss Consul-General will submit a request to the Japanese authorities for cooperation in the arrest. Japanese military spokesmen remained silent on the matter, saying they were unaware of it.

Extortion Attempt; Dong Hehai Sentenced to Imprisonment

Zhang Yinlai, from Ningbo, operates the Zhang Xiangtai button shop at 690 Burkill Road. On the 6th of this month, Zhang received a threatening letter from gangsters, demanding 5,000 yuan in legal tender, instructing him to wrap the money in a package resembling a book, addressed to "Li," and send it to the intersection of Haining Road and North Jiangxi Road, where someone would contact him. The letter warned of consequences if he didn't comply. Zhang ignored the letter. On the 9th, he received a second letter, accusing Zhang of ignoring their warning and threatening the safety of his family if he continued to ignore them. Zhang reported the matter to the Zhabei Police Station, who dispatched detective Ma Zhong and Weng Peiyu to the designated location, accompanied by Zhang's representative, Xia Chengen. At the appointed time, Dong Hehai (aka Dong Ruhai) from Ningbo arrived to make contact and was arrested. A search of his residence at 49, Lane 348, Weihaiwei Road, uncovered envelopes and scratch paper identical to those used in the extortion letters. He was taken to the Police Station. Yesterday morning, he was sent to the First Special Court. Attorney Li Zhishan of the Police brought charges against him. The defendant confessed. Judge Fu sentenced Dong to four months imprisonment and ordered the destruction of the extortion letters.

Daughters of Deceased Fujian Merchant Huang Zhan'ao Contest Inheritance; Request Detailed Calculation of Estate for Fair Distribution; Defendant Requests Dismissal; Adjourned Indefinitely

Huang Linying (38 years old, from Min County, Fuzhou, residing at 7, Lane 164, Avenue Foch), the second wife of the late wealthy merchant Huang Zhan'ao from Min County, Fuzhou, acting as the legal representative for her daughters Huang Ruji (20 years old) and Huang Ruqi (19 years old), has retained attorney Li Zhongdao to file a lawsuit in the Second Special Court against Huang Ruchan (57 years old), Huang Rubi (50 years old, residing at 19, Lane 188, Avenue Albert), and Huang Ruhao (46 years old, residing at 15, Lane 56, Rue Foochow), all born to Huang Zhan'ao's first wife, Ji, demanding the surrender of the late father Zhan'ao's estate and a detailed accounting of the

entire estate,

and requesting that the portion to be distributed be specified and retained. They also request that Zhan'ao's will be surrendered. The facts are that the plaintiff's legal representative, Huang Linying, married the late wealthy merchant Huang Zhan'ao in 1921 as his second wife and had two daughters, Ruji and Ruqi. The first wife, Pan, bore the three brothers, Huang Ruchan, Huang Rubi, and Huang Ruhao, whom are the accused. Zhan'ao owned Hengsheng, Fuyuan, and other cloth shops in Fuzhou, 50,000 yuan worth of shares in the Shanghai Commercial Press, and the Huang Feng 嶰 shop in Shanghai, specializing in Shanghai-Fuzhou remittance services. In recent years, he also engaged in

the cotton and cloth business

in Guangzhou and Fuzhou, and owned over 800 mu of farmland and houses, totaling over three million yuan in assets. Unfortunately, in 1923, Zhan'ao was injured in a tram accident in the French Concession in Shanghai and died from his injuries. After Ruji was born, he made a will to protect the rights of his wife and daughters, with provisions for the inheritance of the plaintiffs. However, the defendants viewed this with jealousy. When the plaintiff went to the hospital to visit Zhan'ao when he was on his deathbed, she was refused by the defendants. When she saw her late father before his death, he could no longer speak. Now the defendants have divided up the estate and the property that the plaintiffs should inherit

has all been divided.

Therefore, the court is requested to order the defendants to surrender the will and report the total amount of the estate in order to present evidence for distribution according to law. The court accepted the case and, yesterday afternoon, Judge Tan Hao opened the seventh court to hear the case. First, the plaintiff's lawyer presented the facts and reasons of the case and the objects of the request. The defendants, represented by lawyer Ma Shouhua, requested that the plaintiff's lawsuit be dismissed. Their defense was that Huang Linying, the legal representative, was Zhan'ao's concubine and not his second wife. Zhan'ao had only made a distribution list for his nephews and three sons and did not make a will. Furthermore, in 1923, women did not

have inheritance rights.

Women only had inheritance rights from 1927. All the estate was distributed in 1925, and the plaintiff signed on that occasion. However, the distribution list only specified the three defendant brothers and that a house was built for the plaintiff at a cost of 10,000 yuan. If she remained chaste, a chastity arch would be built to honor her after her death. The court examined the statements and ordered a postponement, instructing the defendant to submit the distribution list for review before further examination.

Letter

To the Editor,

According to Mr. Lu Zhenqing, Director of the Sino-Western Sanatorium, the news report in the Shen Bao on October 4 regarding the lawsuit filed by Li Yuying's father to recover funeral expenses, contained elements that implicated him. Specifically, the report stated that "Lu Zhenqing withheld 8,700 yuan in cash and gold jewelry and clothing worth 100 yuan left by Li Yuying, refusing to return them to the deceased's parents, which led Li Shizhen, the deceased's father, to file a lawsuit against Lu in the Second Special Court, which is currently being audited by an accountant." However, Li Yuying's belongings were kept in the sanatorium at the request of the China Funeral Home for provisional attachment, and sealed by the Second Special District Court. It was not that Lu Zhenqing was withholding them. The deceased's parents filed a lawsuit for evidence preservation in the Second Special District Court. All the sanatorium's books and records were investigated and verified by the court and returned to the sanatorium. There was no lawsuit in the Civil Court. Past reports in various newspapers regarding the death of Li Yuying were largely inconsistent with the facts. The undersigned, as attorneys, always uphold fairness and impartiality in correcting inaccurate records, not only for the gratitude of Lu Zhenqing alone, but also to ensure that the truth is published for the benefit of society. We respectfully request that your esteemed newspaper correct the inaccuracies. We would be extremely grateful. Respectfully, attorneys Shan Yuhua and Ling Changyan, October 10.

Free Talk

Editor's Note

Regarding the "Where Should Women Go?" question, we are first publishing Ms. Jiang Yihui's "Our Path" today. In this small space, this article may seem a bit long, but we feel that Ms. Jiang's arguments from social, national, family, educational, psychological, and other perspectives are well-rounded and her thinking is quite thorough and correct. We believe that this is a rare work, with every sentence and paragraph worthy of careful consideration by our readers. We will publish the opinions of many other readers after organizing them in succession.

Women

Our Path

— Yihui

I am the mother of two children. Indeed, most of my time is spent on my children. Especially in the first year or two of a child's life, it is almost impossible for me to engage in any responsible work or social activities. In the joy that a mother sees in her children's daily growth, there is an expression of the infinite sacrifice of women! Perhaps some would say that children will grow up, and a woman who aspires to serve society can still engage in various activities in society when her children enter school, right? However, the reality is not as simple as we imagine. A woman who has been immersed in her family for five or six years or more, even if she is relatively willing to work hard, will not easily re-enter the circle of career. Moreover, due to environmental factors, most women have already lost all contact with the society outside the family, right? A woman's life sacrificed in the family is a unique phenomenon of an unreasonable social system. Before the entire social system is rationalized, this phenomenon cannot be completely eliminated, but it can be reduced to a minimum by means of rational child care institutions. Now let us discuss from the three aspects of women's self-development, the needs of society and the country, and the welfare of the children themselves, why women should jump out of the narrow circle of the family and embark on the path of social activity.

Each Has Its Own Strengths

First, from the perspective of women themselves, women's talents, like men's, have their own strengths. Women's interests are not consistent like men's. Some women are better than others at caring for children. Some men have a deeper interest in children than women. At the same time, some women have talents in science, politics, or art that far surpass ordinary men. For those women who are particularly interested in children, we not only agree that she should care for her own children, but also, in order to increase social efficiency, we also agree that she should care for other people's children on behalf of others. Because taking care of one child and taking care of ten children makes no big difference to a person who has special training. In this way, other women, because there are specialists to take care of their children for them, can develop their individual strengths with peace of mind and make different contributions to society. According to educational surveys, the difference in intelligence and interest between men and women, the difference between the same gender is significantly greater than the difference between the two genders. This indicates that there is a difference between intelligence and stupidity among women, just as there is a difference between intelligence and stupidity among men. Why should we say that women's duty is in the home? As Chen Mingjun said, "Managing housework and taking care of children is also a career," but precisely because it is a career, those who engage in this career must have specialized training. We should encourage a group of women who are particularly interested in children to receive specialized knowledge and training in childcare and to take on the great responsibility of childcare for society. This is truly division of labor and cooperation.

Fight Together

Second, from the perspective of the needs of the country and society, women, who account for half of the population, cannot be ignored in any country, especially in China, which is striving for freedom, independence, and liberation. At the current stage of our efforts, every additional person joining the national liberation movement will bring us one step closer to the final goal. The arduous work of building a new China requires the participation of more than 200 million women to be effective. Any attempt to encourage women to linger in the small circle of the family is doomed to failure. Because in the 1940s of the twentieth century, not only conscious women are no longer willing to entrust their fate to the hands of others, but conscious men have also recognized that women's interests are consistent with the interests of the nation and the interests of the public. The women's problem, like the unemployment problem, is one of the problems caused by an unreasonable social system. Women and men no longer stand in opposition. In the struggle for national liberation and the realization of an ideal society, they are partners fighting together. In order to promote the early realization of national liberation, women must be liberated from the trivial matters of family childcare and engage in the great cause of national liberation, serving as the vanguard of the construction of a new China. The women's liberation movement must be carried out simultaneously with the national liberation struggle.

Group Living

Third, we all know that the first few years of a child's life, the so-called pre-school age, has a very great impact on the entire life of an individual. A child's future health, habits, and attitudes largely depend on whether the parents' methods of education at this time are appropriate. From a material perspective, children need sufficient nutrition, sunlight, air, large spaces, and various toys that can exercise their bodies, develop their intelligence, and stimulate their imaginations. However, how many families can provide children with such an ideal growing environment? Speaking of the psychological environment, few parents have ever studied child education and psychology, and they have no understanding of the nature and needs of children. They are either too strict or too indulgent. Children who grow up in such an environment will hardly become well-balanced, healthy individuals. If parents want their children to grow into healthy individuals, it is best to let them grow up in collective living from an early age. Here, the group referred to is the nursery that accommodates infants from shortly after birth to four years of age. In it, there are specially trained nurses, doctors, nannies, and educators. These people understand the problems and needs of children better than mothers. All the facilities and material environment of the nursery are also most suitable for children's growth process. With such an ideal nursery, which mother would not be willing to send her children to be raised by experts for the sake of their happiness?

Run Nurseries

I feel that the problem that urgently needs to be solved at present is not whether women should come out of the family and engage in various social activities, because in today's struggle for national liberation, women cannot but come out to work hard. Our current problem is how to arouse people in society to have a clear and profound understanding of the value of nurseries, and at the same time, how to unite those who already have an understanding of this issue to voluntarily contribute money and effort to launch a nursery movement. We must hurry up to train a group of childcare talents and establish several large-scale model nurseries, so that this great movement can spread throughout Shanghai and even throughout China. (I heard that the Shanghai YWCA will have plans to open nurseries in the near future. This may be the harbinger of a large-scale nursery movement. We hope it will be realized soon.)

Equality and Mutual Assistance

Finally, I want to say that I hope that men do not intentionally or unintentionally harbor feudal "male-centered" thoughts and consciousness. The relationship between husband and wife should be based on the principle of equality and mutual assistance. Wives should assist their husbands in succeeding in their careers, and husbands should also encourage their wives to work hard in their careers. I am not opposed to a wife "quickly recovering her husband from fatigue after work, or revitalizing him from disappointment and frustration in his career." However, husbands should also fulfill the same obligations to their wives, otherwise they have no right to make such demands. At the same time, I also hope that wives and mothers do not only see the family as our paradise. We must broaden our horizons and expand our scope of activities to create a happy future for ourselves and mankind!

Maxims

— Zhou You

The one who has the ability to strive and the patience to persevere is a genius. -- William Livingston

The important thing is not: "How old are you now?", but: "How are you aging?" -- Marie Dressler

Hawthorne's Case

The Homecoming of the Dancing Queen

— By Cheng Xiaoqing

Hawthorne didn't answer, but nodded slightly. He then asked, "I have one more question to ask you. Last night, when your car passed the Lilan's house, besides seeing Zhao Boxiong's back figure crouching outside the short wall, did you hear any other people?"

Yu Gantang hesitated and said, "Nothing. I only saw the lights on in her reception room. —Ah, I remember, it seemed like there was a car parked on the west side of her house."

"What color was the car? Was there anyone in the car?"

"I didn't pay attention to that, I can't say."

"You certainly wouldn't have seen anyone in Lilan's reception room at that time either."

"That's right, I didn't see them because the car was driving very fast."

Hearing this, Hawthorne stood up. "Alright, you can go now. We'll talk about other things later."

Xu San, who had been sitting there listlessly for a long time, also stood up and stretched his back.

Yu Gantang also stood up, his eyes widened, and he said in surprise, "Mr. Hawthorne, are you letting me go free?"

Hawthorne shook his head. "No, I'm telling you to go back to the police station."

Yu Gantang was disappointed again. "Mr. Hawthorne, since you believe I didn't commit the crime, why don't you let me go free?"

Hawthorne's face darkened, and he replied, "Freedom? Is it that easy? Do you now know the value of freedom? But it's too late. You're an intellectual, how could you do such absurd, degenerate, and almost suicidal things? How can you not pay the price?"

Yu Gantang pleaded, "Mr. Hawthorne, now I understand. I'm determined to be a good person from now on. Since I didn't kill anyone—"

Hawthorne interrupted, "You at least had the intention to kill." He turned to the detective and said, "Brother Xu San, take him back to the station. If Detective Ni is preparing to question Zhao Boxiong, please notify me, I'd like to listen as well."

Xu San nodded, then pursed his lips at Yu Gantang, telling him to go first. The young man dejectedly walked towards the door of the office. But before he could walk out the door, Xu San suddenly stepped forward and reached out to stop him.

Xu San said, "Wait a minute, I have one more thing to say. Mr. Hawthorne, Detective Ni instructed me to inform you that Lu Jiansheng has explained why he didn't go to Yangzi last night. He was playing mahjong at another girlfriend's house, located at 9 Dagu Road, surnamed Gan, but this is a secret. When he left, he repeatedly asked Detective Ni to plead with you not to publish his matter in the newspaper. Detective Ni has already agreed to him." (133)

Entertainment World

Recent News from the Film City

— By Sha Wei

A Precious Birthday Gift

Nelson Eddy, the star of "The Merry Widow," spent weeks inserting thirty-nine candles into his birthday cake. Someone must have spread the word, as Nelson received many congratulatory notes and gifts: hundreds of phone calls and telegrams, over fourteen thousand cards, a pile of gifts (mostly firecrackers), and a child who personally brought a gift to congratulate him. When Nelson met the child in the reception room, the child said without hesitation, "All your records are here, I don't need to say anything more, they've already said what I wanted to say for me." It turned out that the child had collected all of Nelson's records from films and radio performances in the past three years, making it a truly precious gift.

A Future Femme Fatale

Rita Hayworth is a very beautiful actress. In the past few months, nearly ten thousand fans have written to her asking for photos. Rita, wanting to avoid disappointing any of them, dug into her own pocket to print a large number of her portraits, dividing them into two types to send out. Female fans received a photo of Rita wearing sportswear with a puppy, while male fans received a photo of her wearing a tight-fitting evening gown, showing her charming beauty. Ah, Rita Hayworth is truly a future femme fatale.

Handsome Boyfriends

Helen Parrish has a hobby of going on outings. These days, Helen is constantly going out with one person or another. Recently, she has been accompanied by two young neighbors, one being the actor Charles Lamarr, and the other being Bert, the son of Edward Arnold. Once, when they arrived in the suburbs, there was only a woman sitting alone at a nearby table. Helen proudly said when she saw this situation, "Look, we have one more." But later, Helen felt a bit embarrassed, because suddenly many young and handsome men were sitting around the girl.

Paulette Has Changed

Paulette Goddard is truly a woman of a thousand faces. A year ago, from her appearance, she looked completely like a female student who was still studying. But since she traveled with Dorothy Dandridge, Paulette has completely changed. She braids her long hair like Dorothy, neatly combing a bun on her head, applying light blue face powder to cover her sun-reddened skin, and applying blue lipstick for evening outings. She completely changed the lively Paulette. It turned out that after that trip, she and Dorothy became close friends, and they dressed up in the same way.

Meat and Nutrition

George Brent in Hollywood was a rare vegetarian. Since his romance with the "Oomph Girl" Ann Sheridan, Ann Sheridan felt greatly dissatisfied with this and directly criticized him for not doing so. George, probably to please her, now includes boiled onions, lamb, and pork chops in his meals. He seems to look stronger than before.

Commemorating Revolutionary Artist Pan Yueqiao (Part 2)

— By Sick Dove

The Battle of Shanghai

In August of the Xinhai year, the Wuchang Uprising broke out. He was in Shanghai, his heart burning. Knowing the strategic importance of Shanghai and that the potential revolutionary force had surged to its peak, after years of preparation, the time was ripe. On the night of September 13th, amidst the bleak autumn wind and rain, he led three thousand people including police and merchants to the Shanghai Arsenal, launching a fierce attack as if facing a formidable enemy. At that time, the people in the bureau had been influenced by the revolutionary forces, and their thoughts were inclined towards the new government, so they hesitated and waited with their hands tied. Yueqiao saw through the opponent's weakness, stepped forward in the face of the crowd, and explained the great cause. Sure enough, in an instant, enemies turned into friends, and they stopped resisting. At that critical moment, Yueqiao detoured to the rear, set fire to start a fight, and cheers erupted. They poured in like bees, with blood flowing everywhere and countless corpses. He led the crowd, advancing bravely, injured in the arms and legs in several places, but his spirit did not diminish. After the entire situation was under control, he returned to the headquarters. He recounted the details of the attack to the crowd, tirelessly, with fresh blood flowing from his clothes, his whole body red, yet he still talked eloquently, unaware of his pain. Afterwards, some praised his courage. He said, "At that time, I had already given my life to the country, and had long forgotten myself. Revolution is a sacrifice, this is nothing." These words were so慷慨激昂. After the matter was settled, Chen Qimei supervised the Shanghai army and awarded him the position of Minister of Investigation. He smiled and declined, still devoting himself to the stage, using his life to advocate and do his beloved drama life.

Destroying the Home to Alleviate Difficulties

At that time, the revolutionary atmosphere had spread throughout the country. In Fengtian, the revolutionary hero Lan Tianwei, due to the failure of the uprising, came to Shanghai to raise military funds. He saw this news in the newspaper and hurried to the inn to visit him. They hit it off immediately. He immediately threw out thirty thousand gold to let him try to carry out great undertaking again. This kind of豪舉 to donate generously was also a masterpiece of his life. He once said that my friend, is for the country, friendship is important, the country is even more important. After the founding of the Republic of China, he was recognized by Li Yuanhong and served as brigade commander, mixed brigade commander, salt patrol commander, unified tax bureau chief, and water police chief. However, because of his upright nature, he repeatedly encountered dangers. He was once controlled by Zheng Ruicheng, and then again faced danger from Shen Hongying. Although he managed to escape from danger, his family property was destroyed from then on. In his entire life, he devoted himself to the revolutionary cause, going forward bravely, indomitable, with both spirit and perseverance worthy of admiration. In his later years, he returned to his old career and dedicated himself to the stage. It can be seen that the official career is complicated, and how can he get the freedom of an actor.

Wu Mei Agrees to Perform on Stage

"Hero of the Straits" was revived yesterday. The lineup is the same as before, but the role of Zeng Hou cannot be performed because Ding Zhima suddenly fell ill again. After "New Art" contacted Wu Mei, she readily agreed to perform the role for a week. Since Wu Mei took over the Mei Long Zhen Restaurant, she has only performed "Min Resentment" at the Russian Theatre once. It is said that this time she agreed to perform on stage because she loves the script of "Hero of the Straits."

Entertainment News

(1) The Great Bell Theatre Company will perform Gorky's play at the Russian Art Theatre on Foch Road on the 13th. (1) "Night of Storm and Rain" (original name: Autumn Night) (2) Children Without a Motherland (original name: A Child's Birth) (3) Seven Monotonous People (because of monotony) adapted by Xu Xingzhi, Mu Ni, etc. Three performances will be held on the same day at 9:00 AM, 3:00 PM, and 8:00 PM. (2) The New Asia Pingju Society, established by colleagues of the New Asia Pharmaceutical Factory, will start broadcasting on the Great Beauty Radio Station (frequency 1140) at 8:00 PM today. The programs are very exciting and are all masterpieces of the factory's employees, such as Liu Sanru's "Imperial Stele Pavilion," Yao Erdao's "Catching and Releasing Cao," Wang Peide's "June Snow," Zhang Junyi's "A Woman's Imprisonment," Wan Yaofang and Weng Yaxian's "Famen Temple," "Great Ascension Palace," Xu Jingzhi's "Sending a Son to Sangyuan," "Qionglin Banquet," and Liu Yijian's "Locking the Scales," "Wenji Returns to Han," etc. Listeners who purchase goods by phone during the broadcast will receive special and valuable gifts. (3) The Fengshe Opera Troupe of Fufeng Company and the Quyi Department of the Miscellaneous Grain Exchange will hold a grand party on the 26th to celebrate the marriage of Cao Fengjie's younger sister.
